\put(100.0253,-212.1069){\fontsize{13.98}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}2.4 Restrictions }
\put(100.02,-227.46){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}E-commerce restrictions are related to factors external to the product, such as the user's }
\put(100.02,-238.9229){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}internet speed, the user's home if it is difficult for the package to go, and the type of }
\put(100.02,-250.4459){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}internet browser used. It can be viewed on both PC and cell phones, but you may have }
\put(100.02,-261.9689){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}incompatibility problems if it uses less secure web browsers. }
\put(58.97803,-273.4318){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(100.02,-284.9548){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Because the product is recent, it will only have the payment method through PayPal. The }
\put(99.9899,-296.4778){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}client will have the option to implement other payment methods so that users have other }
\put(99.96982,-307.9407){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}options to make transactions. }
\put(58.92792,-319.9447){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(100.02,-335.16){\fontsize{13.98}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}2.5 Assumptions and dependencies }
\put(100.02,-350.52){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Due to the nature of the product, downloading your own software is not required to use it, }

\put(100.02,-396.54){\fontsize{9.986151}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- Microsoft Edge }

\put(100.02,-85.08002){\fontsize{13.98}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}2.1 Functional requirements }
\put(94.98,-98.40002){\fontsize{10.98}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}The functional requirements of the software are: }
\put(58.98,-122.88){\fontsize{13.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(98.46,-147.78){\fontsize{12.9261}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}2.1.1 Functional requirement 1 }
\put(130.02,-163.8){\fontsize{10.98}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}It is recommended to use a monitor that has a resolution greater than HD }
\put(130.02,-176.4599){\fontsize{10.98}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}(1280X720 pixels) to display the information correctly when using the }
\put(130.02,-189.1198){\fontsize{10.98}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}software. }
\put(98.46,-215.7){\fontsize{12.9261}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}2.1.2 Functional requirement 2 }
\put(130.02,-231.6){\fontsize{10.98}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}All the servers must always be connected to the database assigned to it, in }
\put(130.031,-244.2599){\fontsize{10.98}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}addition to the backend and frontend servers being running, otherwise, the }
\put(130.031,-256.9198){\fontsize{10.98}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}page will not be able to be viewed or it will not be able to perform any }
\put(130.031,-269.5797){\fontsize{10.98}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}operation. }
\put(98.46,-296.22){\fontsize{12.9261}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}2.1.3 Functional requirement 3 }

\put(85.02,-106.68){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}models.py is a file in an application directory that contains database model definitions. }
\put(85.01999,-118.203){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Models in Django are Python classes that represent tables in the database. Each attribute of }
\put(85.00995,-129.6659){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the model class represents a column in the database table. }
\put(85.00995,-152.5817){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}In models.py of the orders application, there are the classes that will be related to the }
\put(84.99992,-164.1047){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}orders that are generated on the page. The user attribute is declared as ForeignKey }
\put(84.99994,-175.6277){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}because it will be related to an order number, since a user can have several orders. }
\put(58.95798,-187.2108){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(84.99995,-198.6737){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}The order class will store the order that is generated for the administrator once the user }
\put(84.99995,-211.0985){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}has made the payment. }
\put(84.99996,-233.9541){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}The Orderitem class is what the order includes, such as the products, order number, }
\put(85.00999,-246.3789){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}quantity, and total price. }

\put(85.00998,-269.4249){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}The ShippingAddress class will save information about the address of the user who }

\put(70.02,-81.53998){\fontsize{13.98}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}/products/views.py }
\put(70.02,-106.68){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}In the product views, the APIs are created that will serve the CRUD functionality in relation to }
\put(70.02,-118.203){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the products, such as consulting the name, quantity, category, description, and image. }
\put(70.01999,-141.1188){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}This API view is more focused on the page administrator, for example, different APIS are }
\put(70.03009,-152.6418){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}created with PUT, GET, DELETE, AND POST methods. }
\put(58.99805,-164.1648){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(70.04008,-175.6878){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}DELETE: allows us to delete an item from the store. }
\put(70.04008,-198.6035){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}POST: allows you to create a product and publish it in the store. }
\put(70.01004,-221.5793){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}PUT: allows us to replace the information of an existing product }
\put(69.98999,-244.6755){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}GET: with this method, we obtain information about a product from all its data or those that are }
\put(69.98999,-256.1985){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}r}

\put(70.01999,-152.5817){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}State Management: }
\put(58.97794,-164.1648){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(70.01997,-175.6878){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Uses the useCartStore custom hook to manage cart-related state, such as adding, removing, }
\put(70.00995,-187.2108){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}and clearing items from the cart. }
\put(70.00995,-198.4332){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Local states (address, city, postal\_code) are used to store user input for shipping details. }
\put(59.03809,-210.1366){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(70.08012,-221.7197){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Mutation for Creating Orders: }
\put(70.08012,-233.2427){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Utilizes the useMutation hook from react-query to handle asynchronous creation of orders. }
\put(70.0701,-244.7657){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Defines createOrderMut mutation with onSuccess and onError handlers to handle the success }
\put(70.0701,-256.2286){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}and failure scenarios. }
\put(70.0701,-279.1444){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Cart Display: }
\put(70.07011,-290.7275){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Displays a table with information about each item in the cart, including product name, category, }
\put(70.07011,-302.2505){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}quantity, price, and total price. }

\put(70.08012,-325.2966){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Provides a form for users to enter their shipping details, including address, city, and postal }
